Cartesi Official Announcements 08.03.2022 16:59:53
Animation
Not included, change data exporting settings to download.
39.9 KB
Imagine receiving a computer without an operating system. That would be like trying to speak without knowing the language. An OS is like a home inside your computer. Memory, processes, and everything of the computer's software and hardware are managed there. An OS also allows you to communicate with your computer without knowing its language.

The modern world as we know it functions very well, thanks to operating systems such as iOS, Windows, and the world's biggest OS: Linux.

Now picture instead offering a whole new operating system; a place where Python, C++, MySQL, JSON can run wild and free, but for the first time, totally decentralized. This would be a place of a decentralized society fuelled by blockchain; a whole new OS.

Learn more: https://cartesi.io/

Retweet: https://twitter.com/cartesiproject/status/1501195686523510786
